# Write all files
for path, content in files.items():
    with open(path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:

            zipf.write(abs_path, rel_path)

# Generate each pack into its own folder and zip it

for pack_name, contents in packs.items():
    pack_dir = os.path.join(packs_base_dir, pack_name)
    os.makedirs(pack_dir, exist_ok=True)

    for file_name, content in contents.items():
        file_path = os.path.join(pack_dir, file_name)
        with open(file_path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
            f.write(content)

    # Create the zip file for this pack
    zip_path = f"/mnt/data/{pack_name}.zip"
    with zipfile.ZipFile(zip_path, 'w', zipfile.ZIP_DEFLATED) as zipf:
        for root, _, files in os.walk(pack_dir):
            for file in files:
                abs_path = os.path.join(root, file)
                rel_path = os.path.relpath(abs_path, pack_dir)
                zipf.write(abs_path, rel_path)
    zip_paths.append((pack_name, zip_path))

zip_paths

import zipfile
import os

# Define the output path for the full local tool suite
output_zip_path = "/mnt/data/GhostLink_Local_ToolSuite.zip"

# Define all known tool directories to include in the package
tool_root = "/mnt/data/GhostLink_LocalISO_Kit/GhostLink"

# Create the final zipped tool suite
with zipfile.ZipFile(output_zip_path, 'w', zipfile.ZIP_DEFLATED) as zipf:
    for root, _, files in os.walk(tool_root):
        for file in files:
            abs_path = os.path.join(root, file)
            rel_path = os.path.relpath(abs_path, tool_root)
            zipf.write(abs_path, rel_path)

import os
import sys
import platform

TOOL_PATH = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))

def print_header():
    print("=" * 40)
    print("     GHOSTLINK TOOLSUITE LAUNCHER     ")
    print("=" * 40)

def list_packs():
    packs_dir = os.path.join(TOOL_PATH, "packs")
    if not os.path.exists(packs_dir):
        print("No 'packs' directory found.")
        return
    print("\nAvailable Packs:")
    for file in os.listdir(packs_dir):
        if file.endswith(".txt"):
            print(f" - {file}")
    print()

def open_launcher():
    launcher = os.path.join(TOOL_PATH, "Launcher.html")
    if not os.path.exists(launcher):
        print("Launcher.html not found.")
        return

        os.system(f"open {launcher}")
    else:
        os.system(f"xdg-open {launcher}")

        return

    if os.path.exists(launcher):
        webbrowser.open_new_tab(f"file://{launcher}")
    else:
        print("Launcher.html not found in this directory.")

def show_cheatsheet():
    sheet = os.path.join(TOOL_PATH, "Wiring_CheatSheet.pdf")
    if os.path.exists(sheet):
        webbrowser.open_new_tab(f"file://{sheet}")
    else:
        print("Wiring_CheatSheet.pdf not found in this directory.")

    print_header()
    while True:
        print("\\nChoose an option:")

        print("[3] Show Wiring Cheat Sheet")

        choice = input("> ").strip()
        if choice == "1":
            list_packs()
        elif choice == "2":
            open_launcher()
        elif choice == "3":
            show_cheatsheet()
        elif choice == "4":
            print("Goodbye.")
            break
        else:
            print("Invalid choice. Try again.\\n")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

from zipfile import ZipFile
from pathlib import Path

# Create the folder structure for the Gumroad release
base_path = Path("/mnt/data/GhostLink_Gumroad_Release")
packs_path = base_path / "packs"
base_path.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
packs_path.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

# Create a basic launcher HTML file
launcher_html = """
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
    <title>GhostLink Launcher</title>
</head>
<body>
    <h1>GhostLink Tools</h1>
    <p>Select a tool from your launcher script or run manually.</p>
</body>
</html>
"""
(base_path / "Launcher.html").write_text(launcher_html.strip())

# Create a basic diagnostic prompts pack
diagnostic_prompts = """
# GhostLink Diagnostic Prompt Pack
- Check voltage across terminals.
- Identify ground failures.
- Trace intermittent shorts.
- Test continuity with multimeter.
"""
(packs_path / "diagnostic_prompts.txt").write_text(diagnostic_prompts.strip())

# Create README
readme = """
GhostLink: Core Diagnostic Tool Suite

INSTRUCTIONS:
1. Unzip this file to any folder on your system.
2. Launch the tool using your preferred method (e.g., GhostLink_Core.py or Launcher.html).
3. Prompt packs are in the /packs/ folder.
4. No installation required. Offline use supported.

This tool is real. It works. Itâ€™s yours.
"""
(base_path / "README.txt").write_text(readme.strip())

# Zip the whole folder
zip_path = Path("/mnt/data/GhostLink_Gumroad_Release.zip")
with ZipFile(zip_path, 'w') as zipf:
    for file in base_path.rglob("*"):
        zipf.write(file, file.relative_to(base_path.parent))

zip_path.name

'GhostLink_Gumroad_Release.zip'

from pathlib import Path

# Set up tool pack directory

tool_path.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
packs_path.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

# Tool prompt pack
tool_prompt = """
# Electrical Diagnostics Tool - GhostLink Prompt Pack

PROMPTS:
- "Diagnose a no-start condition."
- "Identify fuse or relay failure symptoms."
- "Guide for testing alternator output voltage."
- "Steps to isolate parasitic battery drain."
- "Trace a short to ground using multimeter."
- "Check continuity from fuse box to tail lights."
"""
(packs_path / "diagnostic_prompts.txt").write_text(tool_prompt.strip())

GhostLink Electrical Diagnostics Tool

1. Unzip this file anywhere on your device.

This pack is designed for:
- Car builders

- DIY troubleshooters

# File contents

This toolset is built for real-world field techs, mechanics, tuners, and electrical troubleshooters.
Fast prompts, wiring logic sheets, online part referencing, and smart camera logic â€” itâ€™s built to fix.

Contents:
- README
- Tool Prompt Set
- Wiring Cheatsheet (text format)
- Summary for Gumroad
- Personal Use License

Licensed for personal or shop use only.
"""

prompt_content = """PROMPT PACK - Electrical Diagnostics

1. Diagnose unknown circuit issues with a vehicle from a photo
2. Generate wiring layout diagrams based on symptoms
3. Identify connector and fuse logic using online cross-referencing
4. Rewire logic using OEM-style formats
5. Translate multimeter readings into repair suggestions
"""

cheatsheet_content = """WIRING LOGIC CHEATSHEET

Red/Black = Power
Black = Ground
Yellow = Signal
Green = Sensor Return
Blue = CAN High
White = CAN Low

Use inline fuses and always check continuity before replacement.
"""

summary_content = """Youâ€™ll get:
- Smart prompts that actually solve electrical issues
- A wiring logic sheet that makes sense at a glance
- Picture-based analysis for real-world systems
- Online reference integration (connectors, fuses, diagrams)
- Lifetime updates â€” no fluff, no noise, just results
"""

license_content = """GhostLink Engineering: Personal Use License

This pack is licensed for personal or individual shop use only.
Do not resell, redistribute, or reverse-engineer contents.

Support the creator by grabbing the Supporter Tier to help expand the toolbox.
"""

# Create files
files = {
    "README.txt": readme_content,
    "Tool_Prompts.txt": prompt_content,
    "Wiring_Cheatsheet.txt": cheatsheet_content,
    "Gumroad_Summary.txt": summary_content,
    "License.txt": license_content
}

for filename, content in files.items():
    with open(os.path.join(base_folder, filename), "w") as f:
        f.write(content)

# Create ZIP
zip_path = "/mnt/data/GhostLink_Field_Tech_Pack.zip"
with zipfile.ZipFile(zip_path, 'w') as zipf:
    for filename in files:

        zipf.write(file_path, arcname=filename)

import zipfile
import os

# Set up the directory and file contents for the GhostLink Tool Pack
zip_path = "/mnt/data/GhostLink_Electrical_Tool_Pack.zip"
files_to_create = {
    "README.txt": (
        "GHOSTLINK ELECTRICAL DIAGNOSTICS TOOL\n\n"
        "Thank you for downloading the GhostLink Electrical Diagnostics Tool.\n\n"
        "Included Files:\n"
        "- README.txt: This file.\n"
        "- ghostlink_cheatsheet.pdf: Wiring reference cheat sheet.\n"
        "- diagnostic_prompts.txt: Pre-written prompts for diagnostic use.\n"
        "- branding_cover.png: Cover image for your Gumroad product page.\n"
        "- electrical_reference_notes.txt: Quick access notes and references.\n\n"
        "Use these tools as guides when diagnosing vehicle wiring and electrical systems.\n"
        "Each component is built to streamline your troubleshooting workflow."
    ),
    "diagnostic_prompts.txt": (
        "Diagnostic Prompts for ChatGPT:\n\n"
        "1. \"Interpret this wiring diagram for a 2003 Honda Accord.\"\n"
        "2. \"Whatâ€™s the voltage drop across this relay based on these measurements?\"\n"
        "3. \"Walk me through testing a ground fault in a 4-pin connector.\"\n"
        "4. \"Compare this photo to an online schematic of a Chevy Silverado fuse panel.\"\n"
    ),
    "electrical_reference_notes.txt": (
        "Quick Notes:\n\n"
        "- Always test grounds first.\n"
        "- Voltage drop under 0.1V is acceptable across connections.\n"
        "- Use backprobe pins for sensitive sensors.\n"
        "- Match wire color to system circuit ID.\n"
    )
}

# Create the zip file and add the files
with zipfile.ZipFile(zip_path, 'w') as z:
    for filename, content in files_to_create.items():
        with open(f"/mnt/data/{filename}", 'w') as f:
            f.write(content)
        z.write(f"/mnt/data/{filename}", arcname=filename)

    # Include branding cover image if it exists
    image_path = "/mnt/data/A_promotional_digital_graphic_for_the_\"GHOSTLINK_E.png"
    if os.path.exists(image_path):
        z.write(image_path, arcname="branding_cover.png")

    # Include cheat sheet PDF if it exists
    cheatsheet_path = "/mnt/data/ghostlink_cheatsheet.pdf"
    if os.path.exists(cheatsheet_path):
        z.write(cheatsheet_path, arcname="ghostlink_cheatsheet.pdf")

import os

# Define paths for the new limited trial ZIP package
zip_filename = "/mnt/data/GhostLink_Electrical_Diagnostics_Tool_Trial.zip"
trial_files_dir = "/mnt/data/ghostlink_trial_files"

os.makedirs(trial_files_dir, exist_ok=True)

# Create minimal trial content
trial_texts = {
    "README.txt": "This is the free trial version of the GhostLink Electrical Diagnostics Tool.\nVisit https://ghostlink.gumroad.com to upgrade to the full version.",
    "GhostLink_Prompt_Examples.txt": "- Prompt 1: \"Trace power from ignition to relay\"\n- Prompt 2: \"Identify ground fault near tail light harness\"",
    "Mini_Wiring_Cheatsheet.pdf": "This file represents a trimmed down PDF version for preview."
}

# Write the text content into trial files
for filename, content in trial_texts.items():
    with open(os.path.join(trial_files_dir, filename), 'w') as f:
        f.write(content)

# Package into a ZIP file

    for filename in os.listdir(trial_files_dir):
        file_path = os.path.join(trial_files_dir, filename)
